                    <h3 class="jeg_post_title">
                        <a href="https://androidtvbox.eu/buzztv-6-home-customization/">BuzzTV 6 App Adds Full Home Screen Customization</a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="jeg_post_meta"><div class="jeg_meta_author"><span class="by">by</span> <a href="https://androidtvbox.eu/author/atb_team/">atb_team</a></div><div class="jeg_meta_date"><a href="https://androidtvbox.eu/buzztv-6-home-customization/"><i class="fa fa-clock-o"></i> February 25, 2026</a></div><div class="jeg_meta_comment"><a href="https://androidtvbox.eu/buzztv-6-home-customization/#comments" ><i class="fa fa-comment-o"></i> 0 </a></div></div>
                    <div class="jeg_post_excerpt">
                        <p>BuzzTV has rolled out a major update to the BuzzTV 6 app, introducing a completely redesigned and fully customizable home screen. The update puts layout control directly in users’ hands, allowing them to personalize navigation, content rows, and visual appearance across the entire interface. Rather than forcing a fixed layout, BuzzTV 6 now lets users define what appears at the top of the screen, how content rotates, and how sections are organized. The result is a more dynamic and user-centric experience built around individual viewing</p>
